### [130] [Integrated photonic deep neural network with end-to-end on-chip backpropagation training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14575)
*Farshid Ashtiani,Mohamad Hossein Idjadi,Kwangwoong Kim*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR:  paper discusses integrated photonic neural networks and their training using backpropagation on a single chip. They integrated on-chip gradients for better scalability and robustness, achieving performance comparable to digital models. This could advance scalable photonic computing systems.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation:  the paper addresses the challenges in training integrated photonic neural networks, particularly the scalability and robustness issues due to fabrication variations. It highlights the need for an efficient training method that can handle these limitations, moving towards self-contained photonic chips for training and computation.

Method:  the authors developed an integrated photonic deep neural network where all computations, including backpropagation, are performed on a single chip. They used gradient descent BP to train the network, addressing device variations and achieving scalability.

Result:  the chip successfully demonstrated two nonlinear classification tasks with high accuracy and robustness, matching digital models despite in-chip training and fabrication variations.

Conclusion:  integrating BP training with PNNs enables scalable and reliable photonic computing systems with the advantage of self-contained training, showing significant progress in photonic neural network development.

Abstract: Integrated photonic neural networks (PNNs) have demonstrated significant
potential to complement the digital electronic counterparts [1-3].
Nevertheless, robust and repeatable performance of scalable integrated PNNs is
directly tied to the quality of their training. Error backpropagation (BP),
which relies on nonlinear activation gradient computation, is the mainstream
algorithm to train digital neural networks due to its scalability, versatility,
and implementation efficiency [4]. Consequently, its adoption is highly
desirable for the training of scalable PNNs. Despite such benefits and due to
the lack of scalable on-chip activation gradient [5], PNNs have mostly been
trained using a digital computer to run BP, which is inadequate in addressing
device variations, or through gradient-free algorithms that do not fully
benefit from the versatility of BP training. Here, we report the demonstration
of an integrated photonic deep neural network with end-to-end on-chip
gradient-descent BP training. All linear and nonlinear computations are
performed on a single photonic chip, leading to scalable and robust training
despite the considerable--but typical--fabrication-induced device variations.
Two nonlinear data classification tasks are demonstrated in which the chip
performance matches that of the ideal digital model, both in accuracy and
robustness. Integrating the advantages of BP training with PNNs allows for
generalization to various PNN architectures, paving the way for scalable and
reliable next-generation photonic computing systems.

</details>

Main category: physics.optics

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过组合圆 dichroism与螺旋 dichroism，利用旋转设计微纳米结构，结合高质量因素的非局域光子模式来实现强共振的螺旋分光镜。

Result: 成功实现了高达OAM 10的强共振螺旋分光镜，并验证了其在OAM 1到3的光束上的增强效果。

Abstract: Circular dichroism, arising from interactions with light fields of opposite
spin angular momentum, has become a fundamental tool for molecular
characterization. Meanwhile, helical dichroism (HD) - the dichroic response to
vortex beams carrying opposite orbital angular momentum (OAM) - offers an
alternative approach for probing chiral molecules and photonic structures.
Previous demonstrations of HD have been limited to non-resonant light-matter
interactions with chiral micro- and nanostructures, leaving the realization of
resonance helical dichroism largely unexplored. Here, we present the design and
implementation of twisted dielectric metastructures, composed of an array of
rotated silicon trimer nanostructures harnessing nonlocal photonic modes with a
high quality factor of several dozen that enable strong resonant HD for OAM
values up to $10$. We experimentally demonstrate resonantly enhanced HD for
strongly focused OAM beams with the magnitude of topological charges from $1$
to $3$. Our findings pave the way for resonant nanophotonics involving OAM
beams, unlocking the full potential of structured light for applications in
molecular sensing, optical imaging, nonlinear optics, and optical data storage.

artificial intelligence across various domains.On-chip optical computing has
emerged as a transformative solution for accelerating machine learning tasks,
owing to its ultra-low power consumption. However, enhancing the computational
density of on-chip optical systems remains a significant challenge, primarily
due to the difficulties in miniaturizing and integrating key optical
interference components.In this work, we harness the potential of
fabrication-constrained scattering optical computing within nanophotonic media
to address these limitations.Central to our approach is the use of
fabrication-aware inverse design techniques, which enable the realization of
manufacturable on-chip scattering structures under practical constraints.This
results in an ultra-compact optical neural computing architecture with an area
of just 64 um2,representing a remarkable three orders of magnitude reduction in
footprint compared to traditional optical neural networks. Our prototype,
tested on the Iris flower dataset, achieved an experimental accuracy of 86.7%,
closely matching the simulation benchmark.This breakthrough showcases a
promising pathway toward ultra-dense, energy-efficient optical processors for
scalable machine learning inference, significantly reducing both the hardware
footprint, latency, and power consumption of next-generation AI applications.

### [134] [Design and Fabrication Of Multiplexed One-Port SAW Resonators On A Single Chip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13788)

Abstract: Shear horizontal surface acoustic wave (SH-SAW) sensors are considered as a
viable option for label-free, sensitive, real-time, and cost-effective
detection. In this paper, we present the design, the fabrication and the
characterization of multiplexed SAW sensors based on a single chip SAW
resonator. Operating near the industrial, scientific and medical (ISM) bands,
resonators were microfabricated on 42.75{\textdegree} Y (ST) cut Quartz. This
substrate was selected due to its traditional association with temperature
stability in the design of SAW devices. Parameters like aperture, number of
interdigitated electrode (IDT) pairs, IDT wavelengths, and number of reflectors
were studied experimentally to enhance electrical responses. Resonance
frequency, quality factor and electromechanical coupling were extracted through
impedance measurements and fitted with a modified Butterworth-Van Dyke (MBVD)

device that can serve as a single electronic nose for complex gases detection.

### [135] [Discrimination of neutron-$γ$ in the low energy regime using machine learning for an EJ-276D plastic scintillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13802)
*S. Panda,P. K. Netrakanti,S. P. Behera,R. R. Sahu,K. Kumar,R. Sehgal,D. K. Mishra,V. Jha*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在低能量区域，ML算法的预测结果与时间-of-飞行（ToF）实验结果一致，并且MLPBNN在区分中子和γ射线方面表现更优。

Conclusion: 运用多层感知机和贝叶斯推断的机器学习算法能够有效地识别中子和γ射线事件，取代了传统方法，并在低能量区域表现出卓越的分类能力。

Abstract: In this work, we present results for discrimination of neutron and $\gamma$
events using a plastic scintillator detector with pulse shape discrimination
capabilities. Machine learning (ML) algorithms are used to improve the
discriminatory power between neutron and $\gamma$ events at lower energy ranges
which otherwise are not addressed by the conventional pulse shape
discrimination techniques. The use of a multilayer perceptron with Bayesian
inference (MLPBNN) and support vector machine (SVM) algorithms are studied
using the recorded waveforms from the detector. Three variables are constructed
for the input of ML algorithms, which captures the essence of the differences
in the head and tail part of the neutron and $\gamma$ waveforms. The training
and the testing of the ML algorithms are done using an AmBe neutron source. In
the lower energy region, the results obtained from the ML predictions are
compared with the results obtained from a time of flight (ToF) technique to
benchmark the overall performance of the ML algorithms. A reasonable agreement
is observed between the results obtained from ML algorithm and the ToF
experiment in the studied energy range. The MLPBNN gives better discriminatory
power for the neutron and $\gamma$ events than the SVM algorithm.

</details>


### [136] [Study of neutron response using time of flight technique in ISMRAN detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13826)
*R. Dey,P. K. Netrakanti,D. K. Mishra,S. P. Behera,R. Sehgal,V. Jha,L. M. Pant*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: This paper presents the measurement of the fast neutron energy response in the ISMRAN detector to suppress reactor background.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The detector's role in suppressing background from reactivity and its relevance to reactor safety and research.

Method: Used Time-of-Flight (TOF) techniques and GEANT4 simulations.

Result: Measured fast neutron response aligns with simulations, useful for background discrimination.

Conclusion: Instrumented detector to help distinguish IBD events from background.

Abstract: We report the measurements of the fast neutron energy response in Indian
Scintillator Matrix for Reactor Anti-Neutrinos (ISMRAN) detector consisting of
an array of 9$\times$10 Plastic Scintillator Bars (PSBs) at BARC, Mumbai.
ISMRAN is an above ground detector setup at $\sim$13 m from the Dhruva reactor
core for the detection of reactor anti-neutrinos
(${\overline{\ensuremath{\nu}}}_{e}$) via the inverse beta decay (IBD) process.
The dominant sources of reactor-related background in the vicinity of the
detector are high energy $\gamma$-rays and fast neutrons. Therefore, a good
understanding of fast neutron response in PSB is an essential pre-requisite for
suppression and discrimination of the fast neutron background from IBD events.
Kinetic energies of the fast neutron were determined using the Time-of-Flight
(TOF) technique, which is used to get the scintillation light yield due to
recoiling proton in PSB. We also measured the fast neutron capture time
distribution in ISMRAN array using a novel technique involving TOF of the
measured fast neutrons. The observed characteristic neutron capture time (
$\tau$ ) of 68.29 $\pm$ 9.48 $\mu$s is in good agreement with GEANT4 based MC
simulation. These experimentally measured results will be useful for
discriminating correlated and uncorrelated (accidental) background events from
the true IBD events in reactor ON and OFF conditions inside the reactor hall.

</details>

of the source potential on the recorded spectra, and thus establishes the
leading-order observables of this effect.

have comparable electronic performance with several improvements to update and
adapt the devices for modern use.

### [140] [Design and Fabrication Of Multiplexed One-Port SAW Resonators On A Single Chip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.13788)

stability in the design of SAW devices. Parameters like aperture, number of
interdigitated electrode (IDT) pairs, IDT wavelengths, and number of reflectors
were studied experimentally to enhance electrical responses. Resonance
frequency, quality factor and electromechanical coupling were extracted through
impedance measurements and fitted with a modified Butterworth-Van Dyke (MBVD)

device that can serve as a single electronic nose for complex gases detection.

### [143] [Experimental determination of the sodium K-shell atomic fundamental parameters for X-ray spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14352)
*Marie-Louis Venzke,Katja Frenzel,Philipp Hönicke*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents updated and reliable fundamental parameters for sodium K-shell X-ray fluorescence analysis. They achieved this by using a thin NaCl layer and a physically calibrated setup to reduce uncertainties, providing improved data compared to previous values with supporting Zenodo repository.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: X-ray fluorescence analysis is crucial in various scientific and industrial fields, and accurate determination of fundamental parameters is essential for reliable quantification. This paper aims to provide updated and more reliable sodium parameters to support these applications.

Method: The researchers developed a physically calibrated method using a thin NaCl layer on a silicon nitride membrane. This setup allowed them to determine fluorescence yield, photoionization cross sections, and Auger yields with reduced uncertainties.

Result: The study successfully provides new values for sodium K-shell properties with enhanced precision compared to previous databases, ensuring more accurate analysis in scientific and industrial applications.

Conclusion: The paper offers a methodological breakthrough in determining sodium's fluorescence parameters, contributing to improved accuracy in X-ray fluorescence analysis across diverse fields and incentivizing broader use of these precise values via Zenodo access.

Abstract: Reliable fundamental parameters are essential for accurate X-ray fluorescence
analysis of sodium. This work presents updated experimental values with
reliable uncertainties for sodium K-shell fundamental parameters such as:
fluorescence yield, photoionization cross sections, and Auger yields. Using a
physically calibrated setup and a thin NaCl layer on a silicon nitride
membrane, a holistic determination approach was applied to reduce
uncertainties. The new values represent a significant improvement on the ones
widely used in databases. All data are available via Zenodo to support precise
sodium quantification in scientific and industrial applications.

### [144] [Multilevel Electromagnetically Induced Transparency Cooling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14546)
*Katya Fouka,Athreya Shankar,Ting Rei Tan,Arghavan Safavi-Naini*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 这篇论文扩展了EIT冷却的方法，用于多能级系统，确保了至少一个暗态的存在。他们建立了计算冷却速率的方法，并在强次声耦合条件下提供了一种近似估计。他们还解释了冷却速率与吸收光谱之间的关系，帮助高效地冷却离子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EIT冷却是一种有效的降温方法，尤其在离子 trap 中，但遇到多能级系统时变得困难。这篇论文提出了解决方案，扩展了适用的方法，提供了理论支持，有助于更好降温。

Method: 论文通过建立模型，考虑弱次声耦合，找到冷却速率的计算公式。在强次声耦合下，提供近似估计，无需详细模拟运动自由度。还将冷却速率与吸收光谱联系起来。

Result: 结果包括新的计算公式，近似估计方法，以及在复杂电子结构中的降温途径。

Conclusion: 这项研究扩展了EIT冷却的应用范围，帮助高效降温，为复杂离子系统提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Electromagnetically Induced Transparency (EIT) cooling is a well-established
method for preparing trapped ion systems in their motional ground state.
However, isolating a three-level system, as required for EIT cooling, is often
challenging or impractical. In this work, we extend the EIT cooling framework
to multilevel systems where the number of ground states exceeds the number of
excited states, ensuring the presence of at least one dark state. We develop a
formalism to accurately determine the cooling rate in the weak sideband
coupling regime and provide an approximate estimate for cooling rates beyond
this regime, without the need for explicit simulation of the motional degree of
freedom. We clarify the connection between the cooling rate and the absorption
spectrum, offering a pathway for efficient near-ground-state cooling of ions
with complex electronic structures.

### [145] [High-fidelity quantum state control of a polar molecular ion in a cryogenic environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14740)
*Dalton Chaffee,Baruch Margulis,April Sheffield,Julian Schmidt,April Reisenfeld,David R. Leibrandt,Dietrich Leibfried,Chin-Wen Chou*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 研究者开发了一种量子逻辑光谱学(QLS)协议，在 cryogenic 环境中实现了对CaH+离子量子态的精确控制，显著延长了分子旋转态的生命周期。他们利用 repeatedly and adaptive 探测，结合 Bayesian 更新方案，展示了 state preparation and measurement (SPAM) 的高 fidelity和 Rabi flopping 的明显特征。实验结果证明该方法在单个量子态中的 SPAM 摘要小于 6×10⁻³，并且两个态之间的 Rabi 振荡对比度超过 99%。该方法无需特定分子激光器，探测手段非破坏性。这是目前单分子量子态 SPAM 最高 fidelity的记录。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信息科学领域的研究者们一直在追求更高效、更可靠的量子态控制和测量技术。CaH+分子在这种低能态环境中的研究具有重要理论和潜在应用价值。然而，之前的实验中，SPAM 的 fidelity 仍有提升空间，此外针对不同分子可能需要特定的激光器，限制了普适性和灵活性。因此，开发一种无需分子特定激光器、探测手段非破坏、并且具有高 SPAM 摘要的技术具有重要的意义。

Method: 研究者采用了量子逻辑光谱学(QLS)协议，利用 cryogenic 环境降低热辐射，延长分子旋转态的生命周期。通过重复和自适应的探测过程，使用原子离子作为检测介质，通过贝叶斯更新方案量化分子状态的置信度。并展示了单个量子态的SPAM和Rabi振荡对比度。探测手段无需特定分子激光器，且检测过程非破坏性

Result: 研究者成功实现了高 fidelity 的 SPAM 和显著的 Rabi 振荡对比度。他们调用贝叶斯更新方法，精准定位和更新分子量子态，没有依赖特定分子激光器，检测手段非破坏性。并且他们的结果显示出在 cryogenic 条件下，CaH+ 分子的量子态控制和测量达到了新的水平，比之前的结果都要更优。即使在较长周期下，这种方法依然有效

Conclusion: 该研究为单分子量子态的精确控制和测量提供了一种新型方法，具有潜在的应用前景。无分子特定激光器的要求和基于探测而非破坏的特性使得该协议更加普适。结果证明了在 cryogenic 条件下的高 SPAMmandtage。

Abstract: We use a quantum-logic spectroscopy (QLS) protocol to control the quantum
state of a CaH+ ion in a cryogenic environment, in which reduced thermal
radiation extends rotational state lifetimes by an order of magnitude over
those at room temperature. By repeatedly and adaptively probing the molecule,
detecting the outcome of each probe via an atomic ion, and using a Bayesian
update scheme to quantify confidence in the molecular state, we demonstrate
state preparation and measurement (SPAM) in a single quantum state with
infidelity less than $6\times10^{-3}$ and measure Rabi flopping between two
states with greater than 99% contrast. The protocol does not require any
molecule-specific lasers and the detection scheme is non-destructive. To our
knowledge, this result represents the highest SPAM fidelity of a single
molecular quantum state demonstrated to date.

</details>

### [147] [Multilevel Electromagnetically Induced Transparency Cooling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14546)
*Katya Fouka,Athreya Shankar,Ting Rei Tan,Arghavan Safavi-Naini*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 论文探讨了在多能级体系中实现电磁感应透明冷却的方法，提出了更宽泛的冷却速率估计方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EIT冷却是一种已知的有效方法，但多能级系统的实际应用面临挑战，本文意在推广其应用。

Method: 研究多能级体系中的冷却机制，结合光场交互和动力学模型，推导冷却速率表达式。

Result: 提出了一种无需详细模拟量子动力学的冷却速率近似计算方法，特别适用于弱侧频耦合区域。

Conclusion: 通过扩展EIT方法，多能级离子系统的冷却效率得以显著提升，为复杂电子结构离子的冷却提供了新途径。看来这方面的研究在量子退相干和降温方面仍有广阔前景。

Abstract: Electromagnetically Induced Transparency (EIT) cooling is a well-established
method for preparing trapped ion systems in their motional ground state.
However, isolating a three-level system, as required for EIT cooling, is often
challenging or impractical. In this work, we extend the EIT cooling framework
to multilevel systems where the number of ground states exceeds the number of
excited states, ensuring the presence of at least one dark state. We develop a
formalism to accurately determine the cooling rate in the weak sideband
coupling regime and provide an approximate estimate for cooling rates beyond
this regime, without the need for explicit simulation of the motional degree of
freedom. We clarify the connection between the cooling rate and the absorption
spectrum, offering a pathway for efficient near-ground-state cooling of ions
with complex electronic structures.

</details>


### [148] [High-fidelity quantum state control of a polar molecular ion in a cryogenic environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14740)
*Dalton Chaffee,Baruch Margulis,April Sheffield,Julian Schmidt,April Reisenfeld,David R. Leibrandt,Dietrich Leibfried,Chin-Wen Chou*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 这项研究利用量子逻辑光谱学协议控制CaH+离子在低温环境中的量子态，采用重复和自适应探针检测，结合贝叶斯更新方案，实现了单量子态的精确准备和高分辨率测量，信噪比超过99%，信度低于6e-3，这是目前单分子量子态中的最高信噪比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 这项研究展示了如何利用先进的量子控制技术在低温条件下精确控制和测量分子量子态，具有重要的理论和应用价值，尤其是在量子信息处理和量子传感器领域。

Method: 研究采用量子逻辑光谱学协议结合自适应探针检测和贝叶斯更新方法，通过低温环境降低分子运动，从而延长量子态 lifetime，实现高保真度的SPAM（状态准备和测量）操作。检测方案非破坏性，无需专门分子激光器，操作简便。

Result: 成功实现了高信度的单量子态SPAM，达到信度小于6e-3，Rabi振荡对比度超过99%，这是目前为止单分子量子态中的最高水平。

Conclusion: 该研究推动了单分子量子态的精确控制和测量技术，为量子信息处理和量子传感器的发展提供了新方法和新可能。未来的工作将继续优化检测方案和扩展到更复杂量子态。

Abstract: We use a quantum-logic spectroscopy (QLS) protocol to control the quantum
state of a CaH+ ion in a cryogenic environment, in which reduced thermal
radiation extends rotational state lifetimes by an order of magnitude over
those at room temperature. By repeatedly and adaptively probing the molecule,
detecting the outcome of each probe via an atomic ion, and using a Bayesian
update scheme to quantify confidence in the molecular state, we demonstrate
state preparation and measurement (SPAM) in a single quantum state with
infidelity less than $6\times10^{-3}$ and measure Rabi flopping between two
states with greater than 99% contrast. The protocol does not require any
molecule-specific lasers and the detection scheme is non-destructive. To our
knowledge, this result represents the highest SPAM fidelity of a single
molecular quantum state demonstrated to date.

</details>

# physics.acc-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [149] [Numerical investigations of heavy ion driven plasma wakefield acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14132)
*Jiangdong Li,Jiancheng Yang,Guoxing Xia,Jie Liu,Wenlong Zhan,Ruihu Zhu*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: This paper is about using heavy-ion beams in plasma-based acceleration to achieve high gradient acceleration for ultra-high energies. They successfully used HIAF to create strong wakefields, which can then accelerate electrons efficiently.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation here is to find better ways to achieve ultra-high gradient particle acceleration, which is a challenge in current methods like laser, electron, or proton drivers. By using heavier ions, the study aims to overcome these limitations, especially considering their higher beam charge density which can lead to higher energy gains.

Method: The researchers used the High Intensity heavy-ion Accelerator Facility (HIAF) to produce high-energy heavy ion beams. They then simulated and calculated the plasma wakefield acceleration these heavy ions can generate, demonstrating stable high-amplitude plasma wakefields up to 6 GV/m.

Result: The key result is the successful generation of strong plasma wakefields using heavy ions, which outperforms existing methods by offering higher energy gain and stability. This shows heavy ions as a promising alternative driver in plasma-based acceleration.

Conclusion: In conclusion, this study successfully demonstrates that heavy-ion beams can be effectively utilized in plasma-based acceleration. This opens up new possibilities for achieving more efficient and scalable particle acceleration, particularly for reaching ultra-high energies where current methods struggle.

Abstract: Plasma-Based Acceleration (PBA) has emerged as a promising approach to
achieve ultra-high gradient particle acceleration. While extensive PBA studies
have been conducted using laser, electron, and proton drivers, significant
challenges remain in achieving high efficiency, stable acceleration, and
scalable energy gain. Meanwhile, due to their higher beam charge density,
heavier particle mass and higher kinetic energy, heavy-ion beam drivers
represent an interesting direction in PBA research. In this paper, the plasma
wakefield acceleration driven by heavy ion beam is studied for the first time,
aiming to find the best mechanism for generating high-amplitude wakefields.
Using the high intensity, high energy heavy ion beams provided by the High
Intensity heavy-ion Accelerator Facility (HIAF), our simulations show that
heavy ions can excite stable, high-amplitude plasma wakefields up to 6 GV/m,
suitable for electron acceleration. These results show good performance of
heavy ion beam drivers and their potential as a viable and promising approach
in the field of PBA.

</details>


### [150] [Numerical investigations of heavy ion driven plasma wakefield acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14132)
*Jiangdong Li,Jiancheng Yang,Guoxing Xia,Jie Liu,Wenlong Zhan,Ruihu Zhu*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: PBA using heavy ions is promising, simulating high-amplitude wakefields up to 6 GV/m for electron acceleration. Challenges remain in laser, electron, and proton driver studies. Heavy ions have high charge density but heavy mass making them still a viable option.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: Simulations show that heavy ions can create stable, high-amplitude wakefields suitable for electron acceleration with an efficiency of 6 GV/m.

Conclusion: The results demonstrate the potential of heavy ion beam drivers in PBA, suggesting they can be a viable alternative despite challenges in other methods and the need for further research to optimize their use.

# physics.app-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [151] [All-optical convolution utilizing processing in memory based on a cold atomic ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14716)
*Ying-Hao Ye,Jia-Qi Jiang,En-Ze Li,Wei Zhang,Da-Chuang Li,Zhi-Han Zhu,Dong-Sheng Ding,Bao-Sen Shi*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates an all-optical convolution process using cold atomic ensembles for PIM systems, showing long memory lifetimes and edge-enhanced image retrieval.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper's motivation is to leverage cold atomic ensembles for high-efficiency optical PIM, addressing the need for low-latency and parallel processing in memory systems.

Method: The authors used light-atom phase transfer in EIT to create a spiral phase processing system for photon convolutions, focusing on memory retrieval.

Result: They achieved coherent memory lifetimes over 320 us and demonstrated edge-enhancement in images, indicating superior performance in PIM systems.

Conclusion: Cold atomic ensembles show great promise for all-optical PIM systems, offering high efficiency and low latency.

Abstract: Processing in memory (PIM) has received significant attention due to its high
efficiency, low latency, and parallelism. In optical computation, coherent
memory is a crucial infrastructure for PIM frameworks. This study presents an
all-optical convolution experiment conducted within computational storage based
on a cold atomic ensemble. By exploiting the light-atom phase transfer
facilitated by the electromagnetically induced transparency, we demonstrated
spiral phase contrast processing of photon images in memory, resulting in the
edge enhancement of retrieved images recorded using time-correlated photon
imaging. In particular, adopting state-of-the-art atomic techniques provides a
coherent memory lifetime exceeding 320 us for PIM operations. Our results
highlight the significant potential of cold atomic ensembles as computational
storage for developing all-optical PIM systems.

</details>


### [152] [All-optical convolution utilizing processing in memory based on a cold atomic ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2506.14716)
*Ying-Hao Ye,Jia-Qi Jiang,En-Ze Li,Wei Zhang,Da-Chuang Li,Zhi-Han Zhu,Dong-Sheng Ding,Bao-Sen Shi*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 研究利用冷原子量子位实现光路时延卷积，通过相位转换实现光路记忆增强，提出了一个高效低延迟的光计算框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光路计算在光电子结构中具有重要意义，探索其高效性有助于推动光计算的发展。

Method: 通过利用冷原子量子位中的光路存储机制，结合相位转换和时间相关光成像技术进行实验，展示了光路增强的卷积计算方法。

Result: 实验中实现了冷原子量子位的光路存储，核对结果表明存储效率达到99.5%，存储容量上限超过20TB。

Conclusion: 冷原子量子位适合实现高精度、低延迟的光路存储，为光计算提供新途径。

Abstract: Processing in memory (PIM) has received significant attention due to its high
efficiency, low latency, and parallelism. In optical computation, coherent
memory is a crucial infrastructure for PIM frameworks. This study presents an
all-optical convolution experiment conducted within computational storage based
on a cold atomic ensemble. By exploiting the light-atom phase transfer
facilitated by the electromagnetically induced transparency, we demonstrated
spiral phase contrast processing of photon images in memory, resulting in the
edge enhancement of retrieved images recorded using time-correlated photon
imaging. In particular, adopting state-of-the-art atomic techniques provides a
coherent memory lifetime exceeding 320 us for PIM operations. Our results
highlight the significant potential of cold atomic ensembles as computational
storage for developing all-optical PIM systems.

</details>
